  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_aa03266e-1418-4813-93b7-ee9d3fef5ef5'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText4197578506595184367" style="display:none">Justice North is the face of New Species. Seeing him up close makes Jessie's heart race. He's the ultimate alpha male-big, muscular, exotically beautiful...and dangerous. Of course he's off limits. But then the sexy man purrs and all bets are off.<br /><br />Jessie Dupree is a mouthy, fiery human female who brings out the animal in Justice. She wants to show him how to relax, and he's all for anything she wants to do, but Justice has sworn to protect his people and to take a Species mate. He's torn between the woman he wants and the oath he's taken. <br /><br />Jessie knows a relationship between them probably won't end well; heartbreak is inevitable. But that won't stop her from freeing the wildness inside Justice and spending every moment she can steal wrapped around his hot body, making him roar with passion.<br /><br /><br />Reader Advisory: Each New Species book may be read as a standalone, but we suggest reading them in order to get the most enjoyment from the series.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6687614364592287582"><blockquote>
  
    <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396051521i/9083240.jpg' alt=' photo a9e07b89198d92d7a5b249e0319c4205_zps34f5f5af.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  
</blockquote>I am becoming totally addicted to this series!!!<br/><br/>Justice is the 4th book in this series and met Justice in the previous books, I was so looking forward to his story and WOW…I just LOVED IT!!!<br/>Justice North, breathtakingly gorgeous<img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396051521i/9083241.jpg' alt=' photo justicene_zpsdc0cbdd7.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> and leader of the NSO (New Species Organization), is totally committed to keeping his people safe and will do anything for them even if it means him having to sacrifice his own happiness, which has made him feel very lonely and seeing some of his people findi</span>
  <span id="freeText6687614364592287582" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396051521i/9083240.jpg" alt=" photo a9e07b89198d92d7a5b249e0319c4205_zps34f5f5af.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</blockquote>I am becoming totally addicted to this series!!!<br><br>Justice is the 4th book in this series and met Justice in the previous books, I was so looking forward to his story and WOW…I just LOVED IT!!!<br>Justice North, breathtakingly gorgeous<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396051521i/9083241.jpg" alt=" photo justicene_zpsdc0cbdd7.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> and leader of the NSO (New Species Organization), is totally committed to keeping his people safe and will do anything for them even if it means him having to sacrifice his own happiness, which has made him feel very lonely and seeing some of his people finding their own happiness, has made it even worse. <br><br>Into his life blows Jessie Dupree!!!! Daughter of a pro-New Species Senator, who works in the human task force, that help find and rescue the New Species females that had been given, by Mercile Industries as sex slave gifts to their benefactors, soon turns his life into total turmoil. Funny, caring, sassy, kick-ass (hell, she can take down a few of the bad buys on her own……..)<blockquote><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396051521i/9083242.jpg" alt=" photo images_zps03f4a031.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></blockquote><br>Justice can’t resist her!!! But he knows that it will be dangerous to get involved with a human female and he has always told himself that he would take a woman of his own kind to ensure that there would be no conflict between his people and humans. <br>Justice &amp; Jessie are unable to ignore the feelings for each other, even if it means having to hide their attraction from others. She is the first woman that makes Justice feel at peace with himself….yes, some sweet moments like the massage Jessie gives him to the sensual and hot sex between them!! <blockquote><b>“He hesitated. “We’ve been told we’re larger than typical males.”<br><br>Larger. She swallowed. “I can deal with that. Larger as in ‘just a bit bigger’ or as in ‘that is never, ever going to fit inside me’?” </b></blockquote>Oh, did I mention that Justice does roar (okay, normal for a part lion/jaguar!!) but he also…………<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396051521i/9083243.jpg" alt=" photo unnamed_zps6f4c55aa.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">, YES, YES, he<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1396051521i/9083244.jpg" alt=" photo images6_zpsb8d21c6a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">How sexy is that??????<br><br>Huge obstacles ahead….I loved the way Jessie orchestrated the way of getting Justice to stand up and face his feelings for her!!!!! <blockquote><b> “Let me tell you how it’s going to be, Justice. You don’t tell me who I can and can’t have inside my house. I work for the NSO but my personal life is my own. You lost the right to give me your opinion,” she stressed that last word, “about what I do or don’t do the second you decided you didn’t want to see me anymore. You don’t want me so don’t you dare tell me I can’t spend time with other men.” </b></blockquote>Humor, action, romance, intrigue, great secondary characters (please tell me that we are going to get Breeze’s book!!!)…………in the meantime, next its Brawn’s (who has taken over Jessie’s job) book.</span>

He lives his over worked, very busy life</span>
  <span id="freeText17700461132515765397" style="display:none"><b>3 “Dickish? Anal? Jealous?” stars</b><br><br><b>*Spoilers*</b><br><br><b>“You’re not walking out of my life. You’re mine, Jessie.   <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424855659ra/13809849.gif" alt=" photo 11266615_zpsfirrzkwd.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>“You turned me on. You were small yet fierce. You fought incredibly well.”</b><br><br>WTH????? Ok is it me or was Justice a asshat for like over 50% of the book. I don't know what the hell happened! So Justice is book 4 in the New Species Series, and It was a let down. Justice is the leader of his people. He is the face of New species to humans. He lives his over worked, very busy life under a microscope having his every word and action dissected and splashed all over the news. He is expected to pick a Species for a mate , but it's this little human that makes him burn and brings out all his protective instincts. He wants Jessie Dupree so bad, but can he put his people at risk to have the one woman he loves? Jessie knows she shouldn't want Justice he is her boss, but he is sexy as hell and she just can't help wanting him. What starts out as a little fun in the bed gets complicated when she falls in love with a man that tells her they can't have a future together. Will Jessie get her man or will she end up with a broken heart?<br><br><b>“I admit to the jealousy. If you ever allow someone else to touch you, I will kill him, Jessie. I will tear him apart. Do you understand me?”</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/9750089_zpsybb6fbpz.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424855659ra/13809850.gif" alt=" photo 9750089_zpsybb6fbpz.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><br>Justice:<br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/Justice.jpg_zpsktgswjjm.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I just want to cry..... I loved Justice in the first 3 books and I couldn't wait to get to his book. I had such high hopes that he would sweep me off my feet and I would love him more than ever. I was so damn disappointed in the way he was in most of the this. He acted like a jackass, was a coward about their relationship and just pissed me off most of the time. I mean really Justice she can't be with you because of bla bla bla , but if she is with any other man you will kill him Really? I will give him this he got his act together, but I needed it to be sooner. There was moments when he was really sweet and sexy , but far more moments of him being a Jealous ass and having tantrums. And when he was telling Jessie all the reasons they couldn't be together all I thought was <br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/sarah-marshall-booshit-booshit-booshit_zpshvtwihrw.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424855659ra/13809852.gif" alt=" photo sarah-marshall-booshit-booshit-booshit_zpshvtwihrw.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br><br><b>“I definitely was that. You’re beautiful, Jessie. Did I tell you that?” He stared deeply into her eyes. “You’re the most beautiful thing I think I’ve ever seen when I’m inside you and you are enjoying us being together.”<br><br><br>“I made a commitment to my people and getting involved with you adds to the problems we have.” He took a deep breath and his anger faded to be replaced by sadness as he stared into her eyes. “I can think of a thousand reasons why it’s a bad idea to be with you but I’m still here. You’re my one weakness, Jessie. I want you and it seems logic doesn’t help me stay away.”</b><br><br><br><br>Jessie:<br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/0c903567d6fc701c0cccc1b5d437aa4b_zpsfl5ixo1z.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>I loved Jessie. She was sweet, funny, total kick ass girl. Blunt and brave. She fights for what she believes in and for Justice. I felt so bad for her, I actually ached, I felt her heart break every time Justice pushed her away. She was supportive and understanding and really too good for Justice after the way he acted!<br><br><b>“You stand before those cameras, the reporters, and the world pretending to be totally human but you’re not. You can just be yourself with me, Justice. I accept you for who and what you are. You’re the guy who purrs and growls, gets a little out of control when we kiss and there’s nothing wrong with that.” She pushed forward, her hands flattened on the bed and she rose to her knees. Her gaze held his as she tried to show him she meant every word. “There’s nothing wrong with you, Justice North. I think you’re amazing and I don’t want you holding back with me. I want to get to know the real you, not some image you’ve tried to perfect for your job. You’re off the clock and it’s playtime. I’m going to teach you how to have fun and tear down those walls you’ve built. I’m safe, Justice.”<br><br><br><br>“I’m done, Justice. You didn’t want anyone to know about us because you knew we wouldn’t last. You said it was to protect everyone but I assumed that was for only as long as we were still getting to know each other. How naive of me to honestly think you wanted to see if we had a future. You moved me into the house of your future mate and you just made it very clear you’re set on a Species woman. Well, guess what? Fuck you, Justice. I have feelings. Do you get that?”</b><br><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/e91da799dbf5befceda56a71aeeb6b9c_zpsgao0wkqm.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><br><b>“I want you to swell with my child and I want you bound to me in every way possible.” He stared deeply into her eyes. “I want to do everything to bind you to me in every way. You make me happy.” He smiled. “You make my life complete.”</b><br><br><br>I did enjoy that there was new different bad guys and I will say this Laurann Dohner can write some hella hot sex scenes. The book was a pretty good read, could it have been better? Hell yeah! Did I want to choke Justice for most of it? yes! The book did redeem itself and I got some sweet romance towards the end. Oh well I guess I can't love em all. <br> <br>here is my favorite moment from the book:<br><br><b>Breeze approached the table slowly, glanced at the four males sitting there and put her hands behind her back. She waited until she had their full attention before she spoke. “Thank you,” she said softly, sincerely. “You said he cared for her,” Brawn grumbled. “You didn’t tell me he was obsessed to the point of going feral. He nearly took my head off when I told him I planned to claim her.” Cedar laughed. “He might not have overturned the table or wanted to tear your head off if you’d just said you were going to claim her. Breeze asked to make him jealous to get him to admit to his feelings for the human. You provoked him into wanting to kill you.” Bestial grinned. “I did like the part about taking her home, mounting her and fucking her until she screamed. Justice sure didn’t, but I was amused.” Jaded chuckled. “Yes. Let’s not forget that classic line that finally broke his barely contained control. What did you say, Brawn? You were going to fill her with your seed and plant it? That was a nice touch.”</b><br><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://jessicasoverthetopbookobsession.blogspot.com/2015/02/friday-february-27-2015.html">http://jessicasoverthetopbookobsessio...</a><br></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1463924927" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer1391675482447597809"><b>For the sake of this review, I am going to replace Justice's name with the word <u>Dickhead</u>, because that is what his name should have been. He is a giant douchecanoe and I want to punch him in the dick. </b><br/><br/><i>*prepare for the rage*</i><br/><br/><b>This is the worst book in this series so far</b>. The others have been ridiculous and yet lovable. They should have made me ragequit, and yet I thoroughly enjoyed them. <u>This one made me want to throw my e-reader at the wall</u>. <br/><br/>From the previous books, we already knew that Dickhead w</span>
  <span id="freeText1391675482447597809" style="display:none"><b>For the sake of this review, I am going to replace Justice's name with the word <u>Dickhead</u>, because that is what his name should have been. He is a giant douchecanoe and I want to punch him in the dick. </b><br /><br /><i>*prepare for the rage*</i><br /><br /><b>This is the worst book in this series so far</b>. The others have been ridiculous and yet lovable. They should have made me ragequit, and yet I thoroughly enjoyed them. <u>This one made me want to throw my e-reader at the wall</u>. <br /><br />From the previous books, we already knew that Dickhead was a meddlesome asshole. He didn't respect boundaries and seemed to like to get involved in other peoples relationships. <br /><br /><b>I did not think that I could dislike Dickhead more than I already did when I went into this book</b>. But Dickhead managed to prove just how much of a horrible person he was in his book and made me loathe him all the more.<br /><br />Dickhead falls in love with a human woman, Jessie. <b>She can take care of herself</b>. She can do self defense. She's the only woman on an all male rescue task force that rescues enslaved New Species women. Do you think Dickhead appreciates any of this? Of course not. She is human, therefore she is not good enough for him to mate with for life, because, what would the press think? OH I DON'T KNOW, MAYBE THAT YOU WERE MORE HUMAN THAN ANIMAL AND ACTUALLY HAD FEELINGS?! DID YOU THINK OF THAT YOU PIECE OF SHIT?<br /><br />Sorry for the caps. Actually, you know what? I'm not sorry at all. <b>DICKHEAD DESERVES TO BE YELLED AT IN CAPS ALL THE TIME</b>.<br /><br />Jessie is a fierce woman. She has killed people. She has protected her own team. <b>SHE SAVES DICKHEAD'S LIFE</b>. Do you think any of this is ever fully acknowledged by the males in this book? OF COURSE NOT. She kills three men in order to save her team in the first few chapters, and the men in this novel <b>fire her from her position on the taskforce as a result</b>. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I do not care at all that she got shot while she was on duty, a male in similar circumstances would NEVER have been dismissed from his position. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <b>I HAVE SO MUCH RAGE</b>.<br /><br />But that's not the worst part of the book - I know! You're sitting there wondering, Jess is already raging, how much worse can it get? Much worse.<br /><br />So Dickhead and Jessie are banging and then they can't bang anymore because Jessie is a whinging bitch and said that it was okay for them to keep their relationship a secret, when it really wasn't okay for them to keep it a secret, because, <i>reasons</i>. So Dickhead goes out to a bar and unbeknownst to him <s>molests</s> dances with a girl on the dance floor <i>in view of Jessie</i> and so she decides to dance with another guy. Because fair is fair, right?<br /><br /><b>WRONG</b>. It's totally okay for Dickhead to <s>molest</s> dance with another lady, but it's not okay for Jessie to dance with another guy. Because <i>reasons</i>. <br /><br /><b>FUCK OFF</b>.<br /><br />Oh! And it's totally okay for Dickhead to be all possessive and a domineering <b>ASSHOLE</b>, but as soon as something happens to him and Jessie acts the same way, she gets told to calm down, and when she doesn't <u>she is drugged</u>. <b>WHAT THE FUCK?!</b><br /><br />Add to this the fucking drama-llama bullshit of <i>we can't be together, lets keep it a secret, oh we broke up lets have hot makeup sex, omg what are we doing? I hate you, but really I love you and I just can't express my feelings</i> and <b>I can't even deal with this shit</b>. <br /><br />I feel like this was written by a different person. It didn't flow well, the editing was atrocious and the love story was a <b>fucking joke</b>. I hope Dickhead dies in the series, that would make me happy. <br /><br />If I didn't have people telling me there are better books in this series, I would give this up. <br /><br /><b>I wish I never read this book.</b> <br /><br /><b>1</b> <i>go-fucking-die-dickhead</i> <b>Stars</b><br /><br />Thanks for the buddy read <a href="" rel="nofollow noopener">Aileene</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1541088129" rel="nofollow noopener">Alp</a>!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1391675482447597809" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2688757308862714396">Ruh roh, I'm going against all of my friends' reviews here, but I didn't think this book was that bad. Yes, I was angry a few times and wanted Jessie to move away from Justice because he was being a hypocrite, BUT...<br/><br/>*ducks for cover* I kind of understood why Justice thought he couldn't be with Jessie. He has proved himself to be a guy who thinks of every angle before he makes a move. He understood the huge ramifications that their relationship could have with both the New Species and the humans </span>
  <span id="freeText2688757308862714396" style="display:none">Ruh roh, I'm going against all of my friends' reviews here, but I didn't think this book was that bad. Yes, I was angry a few times and wanted Jessie to move away from Justice because he was being a hypocrite, BUT...<br><br>*ducks for cover* I kind of understood why Justice thought he couldn't be with Jessie. He has proved himself to be a guy who thinks of every angle before he makes a move. He understood the huge ramifications that their relationship could have with both the New Species and the humans - along with the danger to Jessie herself.<br><br>I also understood Jessie's point of view. She thought she would be okay with a casual relationship with him, but then realized she was selling herself short by allowing him to keep her on the "down low". When she found out that she was living in a house that he was reserving for his future mate - a New Species mate, she decided that she didn't want to be his dirty little secret anymore. I thought that was a better decision than being his fuck-buddy.<br><br>Now, as penance for my unpopular opinion, I shall hang my head in shame.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457422698i/18356162._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer754037839" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17264592410429450768"> <i>
  <b>"Welcome to our home. Now take off your clothes. I missed you."</b>
</i> <br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383476275i/6573670.jpg' width='400' height='360' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I'm so glad I didn't have to wait so long for Justice's book. His the type of character you love immediately from book one and wish for his book above all else. And I was <b>not</b> disappointed with his story!<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383476275i/6573671._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Justice North</b>, NSO leader, has big responsibilities towards his people. He was chosen by his people to lead, protect and bring them justice, for all they've been handed from the hands of Mercile industries. His calm and poised i</span>
  <span id="freeText17264592410429450768" style="display:none"> <i>
  <b>"Welcome to our home. Now take off your clothes. I missed you."</b>
</i> <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383476275i/6573670.jpg" width="400" height="360" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm so glad I didn't have to wait so long for Justice's book. His the type of character you love immediately from book one and wish for his book above all else. And I was <b>not</b> disappointed with his story!<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383476275i/6573671._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Justice North</b>, NSO leader, has big responsibilities towards his people. He was chosen by his people to lead, protect and bring them justice, for all they've been handed from the hands of Mercile industries. His calm and poised in the public's eye, appearing non threatening to win the human's hearts. That's until he meets the fiery redhead Jessie, the only female that brings out his inner, animal <i>purr</i>.<br><br><i>
  <b>"What are you thinking about doing that you'll regret?" His gaze searched hers and a long moment passed while he seemed to debate answering. "Touching you." </b>
</i> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383476457i/6573711._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Jessie Dupree</b> works with an assigned task force that helps NSO to retrieve their captured Gift females, still held by the men with past associations with Mercile. Jessie is stubborn and works hard at her job to help those females in need, even at the cost of her life. Thinking to share some work ideas with Justice, Jessie finds herself alone with the sexy Species male, with an urge to help him relax. Addicted to his touch and drawn to the man, Jessie is eager to continue their affair. But life isn't that simple for the <b>leader</b> of New Species. <br><br><i>
  <b>"I've never been attracted to your kind before but I'm drawn to you in the worst way."</b>
</i> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383481918i/6574887._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their relationship seemed impossible, with so many difficult obstacles in the way. As a leader and the face of New Species, Justice has obligations and rules he must follow, to protect those he loves. It was heartbreaking to see him so torn up about his responsibilities and his need for Jessie. And her pain on feeling used and unwanted by someone that can never have her forever. I loved how strong and persistent Jessie was when giving Justice an ultimatum. She didn't give in and accept things half way, it was all or nothing for her. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383480062i/6574483._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I really enjoyed the flow of this book. The author keeps you intrigued and engaged from start to finish. And wanting more on the secondary characters featured in each book. I would have to say, Justice and Jessie are my favorite so far. I <i>loved</i> the build up of their relationship, and the love shared between these two strong and determined lovers. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383476457i/6573714._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Another successful New Species read, that won't disappoint. Go on mates, give this a try xx<br><br><u><b>My New Species Reviews:</b></u><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/717777857" rel="nofollow noopener">Fury (New Species #1)</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/745209000" rel="nofollow noopener">Slade (New Species #2)</a><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/752969770" rel="nofollow noopener">Valiant (New Species #3)</a></b></span>

  <span id="freeText10162757427294851952" style="display:none">DNFed at 65%<br /><br />I'm sorry. I can't continue reading this book any longer. I don't want to waste any more of my time on the thing that totally pissed me off!<br /><br />**Spoiler alert!<br /><br />The first half of the book was great. I lost myself in the story, enjoyed every page, and wanted to know more about Justice and Jessie. Both of them were adorable and their chemistry was flammable. I started to have some hope that this one would be my winner.<br /><br />But then everything began to go downhill in the second half. Jessie started to drive me insane! Justice tried to end the things between them because there would be terrible consequences if he, the leader of New Species, got involved with a human woman. He explained to her that he concerned about his people and he couldn't and wouldn't let them down. She was the only one who wanted to continue this relationship and AGREED to keep it a secret. She seemed to understand all the reasons why they couldn't be seen together.<br /><br />Everything between them went well, until one day, she wanted to stay the night at his house. Justice calmly told her that it couldn't happen because her scent would linger there and the New Species who came to clean his house would know about them immediately. And then she asked him about the house where she was living and he told her the truth that he built it for his future New Species mate. Although he tried to explain to her that it was the plan before he met her, she still went crazy. Suddenly, she thought it hurt so bad hearing about his mate. She was only his f**k buddy. He would leave her one day when he met his mate and that was why he wanted to hide their relationship. He felt ashamed of being with her, blah blah blah... WTH!!! Where was a funny, honest, and brave woman I'd known in the first half? <br /><br />She said she wanted him the way he was and this was him, the man who took all responsibilities upon his shoulders. She always knew that his people were his first priority and she was selfish enough to insist that he must let everyone see them together in public no matter what would happen next. She didn't even care if it would cause the damage to all New Species!<br /><br />This is what he tried to tell her...<br /><br /><i>"I can't go public with our relationship, Jessie. Not even for you." His gaze darkened, anger tightened his features and a soft growl passed his parted lips. "I have an entire race of people who look up to me and who count on me to take care of them. I have to do what's best for them and giving fanatics a reason to target us isn't going to help them one bit. Those humans really hate it when they find out one of us is with a human female. You'd be in danger. You couldn't leave Homeland without being harassed at best, killed at worst. Think of your father too."</i><br /><br />And let's see how well she understood his words...<br /><br /><i>"Get out."</i><br /><br />Arghhh! I couldn't stand Jessie. She ruined the book!<br /><br /><br />--------------------------<br /><br /><br />**BR with my lovely friends <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/4150124-aileene" rel="nofollow noopener">Aileene</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/27279812-jess-j-rex-the-book-eating-dinosaur-nynaeve" rel="nofollow noopener">Jess</a>.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer5897283040876088469">Oh how I love to reread these books from time to time.<br/><br/>I realize that a lot of people have an issue with Justice. And while I may not agree with everything he did, my heart truly went out to him. Here is a guy who is trying with all his might to make a better way of life for his people. He is sacrificing his own happiness for that of his people. He works too hard and too much. Not only that, he has to wear a mask to hide who he truly is. It breaks my heart. He only wants someone to love who will </span>
  <span id="freeText5897283040876088469" style="display:none">Oh how I love to reread these books from time to time.<br /><br />I realize that a lot of people have an issue with Justice. And while I may not agree with everything he did, my heart truly went out to him. Here is a guy who is trying with all his might to make a better way of life for his people. He is sacrificing his own happiness for that of his people. He works too hard and too much. Not only that, he has to wear a mask to hide who he truly is. It breaks my heart. He only wants someone to love who will love him for who he is. He finds that in Jessie but doesn't think he can have her. He has to sacrifice love, something for himself, in order to help his people.<br /><br />I absolutely LOVE Jessie. She is one of my favorite heroines in this series. She is tough and badass but also soft and vulnerable. My heart broke for her too when Justice pushes her away. She deserves someone to love too.<br /><br />This is one of my favorites in the series and I'm sure I'll be rereading it again.</span>

Or he's doing those weird lunge stretches you see guys sometimes doing, you know, the ones that have no idea what exercise is, but they pretend by doing awkward stretching lunges. Pff. It's just all wrong. But the horrible cover fits with the horrible male mc inside. <br><br>I didn't write a review about this when I read it and I won't ever reread this, so we're relying on my memory to recount what I loathed. <br><br>Justice is a giant douchebag asshole squid pellet. He's not only a douchey douche to humans, but NS people, too. He's an arrogant bastard in his dealings. <span id="freeTextContainer11489917126980569386">This book by far is the BEST in this series. I love Justice's story. And Jessie is the perfect yin to his yang.<br/><br/>When it comes to the scope, the main characters, the secondary characters and dialogue, this story is completely on point. It blows the 1st 3 books out of the water on this front.<br/><br/>The emotion present in this one is intense and it just jumps off the pages. I love the chemistry between Justice and Jessie.   <span id="freeText11489917126980569386" style="display:none">This book by far is the BEST in this series. I love Justice's story. And Jessie is the perfect yin to his yang.<br /><br />When it comes to the scope, the main characters, the secondary characters and dialogue, this story is completely on point. It blows the 1st 3 books out of the water on this front.<br /><br />The emotion present in this one is intense and it just jumps off the pages. I love the chemistry between Justice and Jessie. Across the board, it is just white hot. As I said this one was intense with the emotion. Reading the story, the journey with Justice &amp; Jessie just held me and kept me enthralled. But the suspense/drama was well thought out. Well executed. And the ending I love as well.<br /><br />What you are presented with in this story and how it all comes together is done smoothly and ends quite nicely. I could not be moved from my laptop. I did not want this one to end.<br /><br />Although I like all the books so far in this series, this one by far was the best for me. So I highly recommend this read. But I would still advise you to read this series in order.</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer740990623" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer2550260146840438534"><b>WOWZAAAA for the hottest of the new species!</b><br/><br/>Meet Justice North, the leader of New Species Organization (NSO)<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382014568i/5573793._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This man knows how to push my buttons. He growled, he roared..and <b>HE PURRED</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382014568ra/5573794.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Justice is a workaholic, considering he's the leader of the new species, he's like a president in our world. The welfare of all his people were on his shoulders and he felt as the leader he had to set examples, including on who he chose to be his mate. He were set that he had to take a new species to be his mate. We</span>
  <span id="freeText2550260146840438534" style="display:none"><b>WOWZAAAA for the hottest of the new species!</b><br><br>Meet Justice North, the leader of New Species Organization (NSO)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382014568i/5573793._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This man knows how to push my buttons. He growled, he roared..and <b>HE PURRED</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382014568ra/5573794.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Justice is a workaholic, considering he's the leader of the new species, he's like a president in our world. The welfare of all his people were on his shoulders and he felt as the leader he had to set examples, including on who he chose to be his mate. He were set that he had to take a new species to be his mate. Well, if it could be that easy...<br>Enter Jessie Dupree. She worked in a task force for the NSO. She's a badass but she's all woman! I adore her!!! These two met and their world was set on fire instantly. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382016109ra/5577254.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Justice was torn between wanting Jessie and his responsibility to his people. There were new species who still bore hatred to humans and humans who condemned the new species..all of them could endanger Jessie's life. He decided to keep their relationship away from public. Jessie wouldn't want that, it's all or nothing. She refused to be a secret in their relationship. Now, have I said I love this girl?<br><br>It's HOT to see Justice in his jealousy, he's feral. He's such a jackass, it's fun to see Jessie drove him to madness.<br><br>How I love this book! This is the best so far. For me this book made up what the previous lacked off, the chemistry is off the chart, it's fun, engaging, emotional, good plots, and I don't need to say it again, it's <b>HOT</b>. Even the side characters were necessary, I want more of them..Breeze, Tiger, Brawn! Well, he's next so off I go. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You make me happy, Jessie. I'm so glad you came into my life. You're a breath of sunshine in the dark stillness my life has become."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You just rock my world and my headboard."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15878902340291136123">5 Justice Stars <br/><br/>Continuing this series I forget how much I love it. Justice is a character who I never really put much thought into if I am being honest. So when this was book 4 I was like Meh but it’s so good.<br/><br/>You don’t think his job would be as hard as it is, he never shows how much work it is to his people.   <span id="freeText15878902340291136123" style="display:none">5 Justice Stars <br /><br />Continuing this series I forget how much I love it. Justice is a character who I never really put much thought into if I am being honest. So when this was book 4 I was like Meh but it’s so good.<br /><br />You don’t think his job would be as hard as it is, he never shows how much work it is to his people. But Jessie when she comes into his life she sees what others don’t see. She sees that he can’t be himself. He has to be the face of New Species.<br /><br />Justice doesn't take time for himself; he works almost 24/7 because the cause is so important. It’s for his people but there has to be balance and Jessie kid of knocks him on his butt. She stirs up emotions in him and he fears for her the more his feelings grow for her.<br /><br />She is fierce and protective, and so is Justice they just click. <br />Fabulous audio can’t wait to continue the series.<br /><br />*You don't have to like my review but its 100% my opinion, and I am allowed to have it.*</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1215589128" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9592958235715658292"><br/><b>RATING: 1-1.5 "Whatever" Hearts</b><br/><br/>Well, Laurann Dohner seems to have a trend going on with this series, in that it goes up and down. I was exciting to read Justice's book, and I think given my rating, it is safe to say, <i>Justice</i> was a HUGE let down. When you have so much hype built on one character in a series, it creates certain expectations, and living up to those expectations is just part of the package deal. And that is what this fails in, regrettably. <br/><br/>Admittedly, this book starts off rather int</span>
  <span id="freeText9592958235715658292" style="display:none"><br /><b>RATING: 1-1.5 "Whatever" Hearts</b><br /><br />Well, Laurann Dohner seems to have a trend going on with this series, in that it goes up and down. I was exciting to read Justice's book, and I think given my rating, it is safe to say, <i>Justice</i> was a HUGE let down. When you have so much hype built on one character in a series, it creates certain expectations, and living up to those expectations is just part of the package deal. And that is what this fails in, regrettably. <br /><br />Admittedly, this book starts off rather interestingly and enjoyable, and with the same charm as some previously well-liked books in the series, but somewhere along the way, it just dies down. There is no "real" story in this, and everything about this book is contradicting. Justice is supposedly this strong, smart and commanding character (hence my excitement over his book), yet, in this, we get nothing but a wimpy and weak personality. Jessie, although funny, didn't seem as strong as previous heroines. Bring these two together, and there is no spark, no magic, only lust, lust and more lust. I was expecting someone so much better than Jessie for Justice, someone headstrong, and <i>worthy</i> of his character, and that is yet another aspect in which I was sorely disappointed. The gist of it is, these two weren't believable as a couple. I didn't understand their sudden "love" or lust for each other, and I sure as heck did not believe their HEA. <br /><br />One thing I've appreciated with this series, is that even though we essentially have men who have been tortured by humans, we always get a plausible romance when they fall in love with a human. Cliche, yes, but it works. This book, unfortunately, featured no aspects that were even remotely feasible, so Justice ending up with Jessie, didn't make sense to me. I felt no connection with them, and quite frankly didn't care about them. <i>They</i> just didn't work together. <br /><br />In general, the plot is bad, the writing is just meh, and the characters are also bad. For example: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Justice giving up control during sex because Jessie wants him too?? What happened to the badass alpha male? Now, its all about his woman. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> *queue eye rolls*<br /><br />Or this: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[At the end, something bad happens to Justice, and he is recovering from surgery, but as soon as he wakes up, they end up having sex together? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Give me a fucking break, please.<br /><br />So, not much good to say about this one, and it might be the worst book in the series, IMO. The only good thing here were the appearances of previous couples and characters I love. Sadly, <i>Justice</i> did have a lot of potential, but it is seriously misguided. I'm going to be reading the next in the series, and if the ratings continue like this, I don't think I'll continue with it. <u>Brawn</u> don't let me down, <i>please!</i>! <br /><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Posted: March 9, 2015</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="9592958235715658292" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3095920974" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2268211561701463875"><b>3 Re-Readable & Cosy Stars</b><br/><br/>Justice North is the face of New Species, elected by his people to be there voice, every decision he makes is with consideration of his people first, and him last. When he meets human Jessie Dupree she has his blood heating and his protective instincts coming to the fore, the problem is that his desires go against what he feels he should do, find a New Species mate.<br/><br/>I like Jessie’s fierce and her ability to kickass, she may be human but she shows a human that represents </span>
  <span id="freeText2268211561701463875" style="display:none"><b>3 Re-Readable &amp; Cosy Stars</b><br /><br />Justice North is the face of New Species, elected by his people to be there voice, every decision he makes is with consideration of his people first, and him last. When he meets human Jessie Dupree she has his blood heating and his protective instincts coming to the fore, the problem is that his desires go against what he feels he should do, find a New Species mate.<br /><br />I like Jessie’s fierce and her ability to kickass, she may be human but she shows a human that represents humanity well. <br /><br />Justice does always irk me in how he treats his relationship with Jessie, ok if I take a step back, I can get why he would think he couldn’t be with Jessie, but…still, was hoping for better from him (a feeling that doesn’t go away in any of my re-reads). <br /><br />I liked how one Jessie realised that she was <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[selling herself short by going along with being his secret and then when she realises the plans he’s made for his future mate, she refuses to continue being, what for her starts to feel like, a dirty little secret. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Overall, this remains an enjoyable read, even if it isn’t one of my favourites in the series, and I don’t see it being removed from my kindle any time soon, if ever.</span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12863677222831820276">This book made me warm up a little more to the New Species Series. Admittedly, I did start with bk #7; then I went back and started at square one. <br/><br/>I know each of these stories will be about a Species finding his or her mate while adjusting to their sovereign homeland and to outside threats against their kind. However, Justice being the figurehead of the New Species is THAT character, the one who you just want to have a great story. His position of being a generally accepted <i>and not quite human</i> p</span>
  <span id="freeText12863677222831820276" style="display:none">This book made me warm up a little more to the New Species Series. Admittedly, I did start with bk #7; then I went back and started at square one. <br><br>I know each of these stories will be about a Species finding his or her mate while adjusting to their sovereign homeland and to outside threats against their kind. However, Justice being the figurehead of the New Species is THAT character, the one who you just want to have a great story. His position of being a generally accepted <i>and not quite human</i> politician, an animal with a cool head, means he must perceive his actions by always having the best interest of his people at the forefront. This conflict evokes legitimate concern on whether or not his mating a human female, Jessie Dupree, will stagger the New Species' cause and sever some of their important relations with the U.S. government &amp; society.<br><br>I felt like this conflict worked deliciously against Justice's dominant nature that demanded he claim his mate. It made for some explosive and sometimes comical situations.<br><br>All in all, Justice and Jessie were depicted as a very compatible couple. Justice needed a strong and fierce mate, and that is sure as hell what he got! The ending was awesome.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383266197ra/6468201.gif" width="240" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Steam</b>: 3.5-4</span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText3657549080754811263" style="display:none">I really kinda liked this one! Mostly because of Justice...i've liked Justice since he was first introduced in book 1...he's soooo sweet and i think he found a worthy "mate" in Jessie..she was a tough heroine, which i liked! This one had a lot of angsty back and forth inner "battles" between the two of them...mostly on Justice's part...which can drive people nutty...but i like it...adds to the drama! LOL! ;)<br /><br />This series is EXTREMELY SIMILAR to Lora Leigh's Breeds and although not as well written, they are still keeping me very entertained and i'll definitely continue reading future books. There have been too many characters that have been introduced that i'm looking forward to reading books about for me to stop now!...Tiger, who is SO funny, Brass, Flame, 927 (from Valiant's book),Breeze and now Brawn who was quite hilarious in his small part in this book...i'm now very much looking forward to his book which is up next!</span>

  <span id="freeText6960028436676096227" style="display:none"><b>Re-read Review March 23, 2017</b><br /><br />Still love it!<br /><br /><b>Original review November 10, 2013</b><br /><br />I think Justice is the sexist man alive and Jessie is the best female character written in a paranormal romance book. <span id="freeTextContainer880712464975355983">Justice let me down. I had such high hopes based on his character in the prior books. The 3 stars is generous. He totally pissed me off. Indecisive and a cheater. Awesome. No he did not have sex. But he took another female out on a date (after having lots of sex with Jessie) and was dancing with her in a suggestive manner and she thought she was getting laid. (This is why it rates as a Safe with Exceptions) It was forgiven too easily. All of his shit was forgiven too easily. Jessie rocked. I lov</span>
  <span id="freeText880712464975355983" style="display:none">Justice let me down. I had such high hopes based on his character in the prior books. The 3 stars is generous. He totally pissed me off. Indecisive and a cheater. Awesome. No he did not have sex. But he took another female out on a date (after having lots of sex with Jessie) and was dancing with her in a suggestive manner and she thought she was getting laid. (This is why it rates as a Safe with Exceptions) It was forgiven too easily. All of his shit was forgiven too easily. Jessie rocked. I love these heroines. </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('tMskZ4C9N+7CBx/KWJ5Cx/teSlfqz+wpsJdgmPcGGgEOmu5z2F+kRr8n0i/H8lSGyKSdyQX9/diJs9maJSYXIw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('fPJTpE2a78nMyDunW8FX9k31Yrz+9ZWVop4PQAAi8mXGo5mwFXh8YbHo9kLErUG3fg+1IhHHhGSburZC0gL/Rw==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer18066719113786793611">I had a rather short area here telling a little about me but then I had more than a few people ask me to expand it so... here goes. LOL. I'm a full time home 'supervisor' which is a nice word for saying I'm a housewife. I'm married happily, I met my dream guy 20 years ago, and we have 4 children. I live in Southern California and I can't function without iced coffee. I believe in romance, I've alw</span>
  <span id="freeText18066719113786793611" style="display:none">I had a rather short area here telling a little about me but then I had more than a few people ask me to expand it so... here goes. LOL. I'm a full time home 'supervisor' which is a nice word for saying I'm a housewife. I'm married happily, I met my dream guy 20 years ago, and we have 4 children. I live in Southern California and I can't function without iced coffee. I believe in romance, I've always been a daydreamer, and I'm a HUGE fan of books, always have been.<br /><br />No, I didn't know that I always wanted to write. I inhaled books as a child. I read entire series (Pippi Longstocking, Nancy Drew and The Hardy Boys, Trixie Beldon, The Borrowers, etc) in a matter of days at a time. By the time I was nine years old I had an adult library card where I visited often. I moved on to John Saul, Stephen King, Richard Laymon, Agatha Christie, and then found romance. I was hooked. I wrote poetry in my teens and then moved on to short stories. My first book was started after I read a real bomb of a book that ticked me off with really horrible characters and a plot that was shabby at best and I thought... I could do better. LOL.<br /><br />I wrote my first book which will probably never see the light of day in the early 90's. I wrote a series of a few books from it. I'm a series fan! I kept writing for fun, wrote MANY books and then in 2009 I decided to try to get published. I wrote my first Sci Fi romance and Ral's Woman came to be. I submitted it and with a little tweaking, Ellorascave sent me an acceptance letter. It was kind of a 'Cinderella' experience for me. It's been a terrific ride so far and I'm really happy that I finally had the time to commit to writing full time. It's a dream come true.</span>
